# GTA SA Moonloader — Complete AI Reference

> Use this file as the single authoritative reference when writing Moonloader Lua scripts for GTA San Andreas.
> **Never guess opcodes or signatures** — only use what is listed here.
> When a function is not in Moonloader base, check MoonAdditions or MoonPlus sections.

---
## 1. MOONLOADER — Opcodes & Functions

Syntax: `function_name(<params>)` → `return_type` — description

---
## 2. MoonAdditions — Extended Functions

### General

- `Creates new quaternion object from the Euler angles.` → `nil` — MoonAdditions
- `local mad = require('MoonAdditions')` — add MoonAdditions require
- `bone.matrix` → `Matrix matrix` — MoonAdditions

- `mps.is_vehicle_pointer_valid(<uint address>)` → `bool` — MoonPlus — Vehicle
- `mps.ped.from_memory(<uint address>)` → `ped` — MoonPlus — Ped | Creates a ped object from a raw memory address.
- `mps.physical.from_memory(<uint address>)` → `physical` — MoonPlus — Physical | Creates a physical object from a raw memory address.
- `mps.placeable.from_memory(<uint address>)` → `placeable` — MoonPlus — Placeable | Creates a placeable object from a raw memory address.
- `mps.release_weather()` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Weather | Releases any forced weather, returning control to the game's weather system.
- `mps.reset_wheel_spin_values()` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Vehicle (global) | Resets wheel spin rate parameters to their default values.
- `mps.set_air_resistance(<float resistance>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Vehicle (global) | Sets the global air resistance multiplier.
- `mps.set_bike_wheel_turn_force(<float force>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Vehicle (global) | Sets the global bike wheel turning force.
- `mps.set_current_weather(<uint type>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Weather | Sets the current active weather type. Use weather_type enum.
- `mps.set_extinguisher_aim_angle(<float angle>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Sets the aim angle for the fire extinguisher weapon.
- `mps.set_forced_weather(<uint type>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Weather | Forces a specific weather type. Use weather_type enum.
- `mps.set_next_weather(<uint type>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Weather | Sets the next weather type to transition into. Use weather_type enum.
- `mps.set_pellets_collision_scale(<float scale>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Sets the collision scale multiplier for shotgun pellets.
- `mps.set_player_aim_scale(<float scale>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Sets the player aiming reticule scale multiplier.
- `mps.set_shotgun_pellets_count(<int count>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Sets the number of pellets per shotgun shot. Max is 16 — higher values will crash the game.
- `mps.set_shotgun_spread(<float spread>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Sets the shotgun pellet spread value.
- `mps.set_spas_pellets_count(<uint count>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Sets the number of pellets per SPAS-12 shot.
- `mps.set_wheel_spin_loss(<float loss>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Vehicle (global) | Sets the global wheel spin loss value.
- `mps.set_wheel_spin_values(<float target_rate>, <float in_air_target_rate>, <float rise_rate>, <float fall_rate>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Vehicle (global) | Sets the global wheel spin rate parameters for all vehicles.
- `mps.sound.from_memory(<uint address>)` → `sound` — MoonPlus — Sound | Creates a sound object from a raw memory address.
- `mps.transmission.from_memory(<uint address>)` → `transmission` — MoonPlus — Transmission | Creates a transmission object from a raw memory address.
- `mps.vehicle.from_memory(<uint address>)` → `vehicle` — MoonPlus — Vehicle | Creates a vehicle object from a raw memory address.
- `mps.weapon.from_memory(<uint address>)` → `weapon` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Creates a weapon object from a raw memory address.
- `mps.weapon.from_ped(<uint ped_ptr>, <uint weapon_slot>)` → `weapon` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Use weapon_slot enum.
- `mps.weather.get()` → `weather` — MoonPlus — Weather
- `<ped>:clear_weapons()` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Ped | Removes all weapons from the ped.
- `<ped>:get_vehicle_pointer()` → `uint` — MoonPlus — Ped
- `<ped>:is_aiming()` → `bool` — MoonPlus — Ped
- `<ped>:is_firing()` → `bool` — MoonPlus — Ped
- `<ped>:is_standing()` → `bool` — MoonPlus — Ped
- `<physical>:apply_move_force(<vector3d force>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Physical | Applies a movement force vector to the physical object.
- `<physical>:apply_turn_force(<vector3d force>, <vector3d velocity>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Physical | Applies a turning force to the object at the given velocity offset.
- `<physical>:get_friction_turn_speed()` → `vector3d` — MoonPlus — Physical
- `<physical>:get_kinetic_energy()` → `float` — MoonPlus — Physical
- `<physical>:skip_physics()` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Physical | Skips physics simulation for this object for the current frame.
- `<placeable>:get_forward_vector()` → `vector3d` — MoonPlus — Placeable
- `<placeable>:get_matrix()` → `matrix` — MoonPlus — Placeable
- `<placeable>:get_orientation()` → `vector3d` — MoonPlus — Placeable
- `<placeable>:get_right_vector()` → `vector3d` — MoonPlus — Placeable
- `<placeable>:get_top_vector()` → `vector3d` — MoonPlus — Placeable
- `<placeable>:is_within_area_2d(<float x1>, <float y1>, <float x2>, <float y2>)` → `bool` — MoonPlus — Placeable
- `<placeable>:is_within_area_3d(<float x1>, <float y1>, <float z1>, <float x2>, <float y2>, <float z2>)` → `bool` — MoonPlus — Placeable
- `<placeable>:set_matrix_scale(<float scale>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Placeable | Scales the transformation matrix of the placeable object.
- `<sound>:calculate_frequency()` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Sound | Calculates the sound's frequency based on its speed property.
- `<sound>:stop()` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Sound | Stops the sound from playing.
- `<sound>:update_frequency()` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Sound | Applies the calculated frequency to the sound stream.
- `<transmission>:calculate_acceleration(<float gas>, <uint gear>, <float gear_change_count>, <float speed>, <float unk1>, <float unk2>, <bool all_wheels_on_ground>, <uint handling_cheat>)` → `float` — MoonPlus — Transmission | Calculates the acceleration force for the given engine/gear/speed state.
- `<transmission>:calculate_gear(<float speed>, <int current_gear>)` → `uint` — MoonPlus — Transmission | Calculates which gear the vehicle should be in given the current speed and gear.
- `<transmission>:get_gear(<uint gear>)` → `gear` — MoonPlus — Transmission
- `<vehicle>:blow_up(<uint damager_pointer>, <uint hide_explosion>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Vehicle | Blows up the vehicle. Note: if you are inside the vehicle this may crash the game.
- `<vehicle>:get_audio()` → `vehicle_audio` — MoonPlus — Vehicle
- `<vehicle>:get_contact_wheels_count()` → `int` — MoonPlus — Vehicle
- `<vehicle>:get_flying_handling_pointer()` → `uint` — MoonPlus — Vehicle
- `<vehicle>:get_move_direction()` → `float` — MoonPlus — Vehicle
- `<vehicle>:get_transmission()` → `transmission` — MoonPlus — Vehicle
- `<vehicle>:get_wheel_position(<uint wheel>)` → `float` — MoonPlus — Vehicle | Use wheel_enum: FRONT_LEFT=0, REAR_LEFT=1, FRONT_RIGHT=2, REAR_RIGHT=3.
- `<vehicle>:get_wheel_rotation(<uint wheel>)` → `float` — MoonPlus — Vehicle | Use wheel_enum: FRONT_LEFT=0, REAR_LEFT=1, FRONT_RIGHT=2, REAR_RIGHT=3.
- `<vehicle>:get_wheel_speed(<uint wheel>)` → `float` — MoonPlus — Vehicle | Use wheel_enum: FRONT_LEFT=0, REAR_LEFT=1, FRONT_RIGHT=2, REAR_RIGHT=3.
- `<vehicle>:get_wheel_state(<uint wheel>)` → `int` — MoonPlus — Vehicle | Use wheel_enum. Returns wheel_state: NORMAL=0, SPINNING=1, SKIDDING=2, FIXED=4.
- `<vehicle>:get_wheel_suspension_compression(<uint wheel>)` → `float` — MoonPlus — Vehicle | Use wheel_enum: FRONT_LEFT=0, REAR_LEFT=1, FRONT_RIGHT=2, REAR_RIGHT=3.
- `<vehicle>:get_wheel_width()` → `float` — MoonPlus — Vehicle
- `<vehicle>:tell_to_go_to(<float x>, <float y>, <float z>, <float altitude_min>, <float altitude_max>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Vehicle | Instructs the vehicle (e.g. helicopter) to fly toward the given coordinates within the altitude range.
- `<weapon>:fire_area_effect(<uint firing_entity_ptr>, <vector3d origin>, <uint target_ptr>, <vector3d target>)` → `bool` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Fires an area-effect weapon (e.g. RPG) from the entity at the target.
- `<weapon>:fire_instant_hit_from_car(<uint vehicle_ptr>, <bool left_side>, <bool right_side>)` → `bool` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Fires an instant-hit weapon from a vehicle, specifying which side.
- `<weapon>:fire_sniper(<uint creator_address>, <uint victim_address>, <vector3d target>)` → `bool` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Fires a sniper-type shot from the creator toward the target position.
- `<weapon>:is_two_handed()` → `bool` — MoonPlus — Weapon
- `<weapon>:reload(<uint owner_address>)` → `nil` — MoonPlus — Weapon | Reloads the weapon for the given owner ped.

## 4. ImGui — UI Library


ImGui is used for creating in-game menus and windows.
Always wrap ImGui calls inside a coroutine with `wait(0)` in the loop.

## 5. Lua Standard Library (Moonloader context)

- `_G(<...>)` — 5.1,5.2,5.3 | _G
- `_VERSION(<...>)` — 5.1,5.2,5.3 | _VERSION
- `assert(<v><[, message]>)` — 5.1,5.2,5.3 | assert()
- `bit32.arshift(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.arshift (x, disp)
- `bit32.band(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.band (...)
- `bit32.bnot(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.bnot (x)
- `bit32.bor(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.bor (...)
- `bit32.btest(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.btest (...)
- `bit32.bxor(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.bxor (...)
- `bit32.extract(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.extract (n, field [, width])
- `bit32.lrotate(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.lrotate (x, disp)
- `bit32.lshift(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.lshift (x, disp)
- `bit32.replace(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.replace (n, v, field [, width])
- `bit32.rrotate(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.rrotate (x, disp)
- `bit32.rshift(<...>)` — 5.2 | bit32.rshift (x, disp)
- `break` — use to break loops
- `collectgarbage(<[opt]><[, arg]>)` — 5.1,5.2,5.3 | collectgarbage()
- `coroutine.create( <function> )` — 5.1,5.2,5.3 | coroutine.create
- `coroutine.isyieldable( )` — 5.3 | coroutine.isyieldable
- `coroutine.resume( <co><[, val1, ···]> )` — 5.1,5.2,5.3 | coroutine.resume
